Here is the script to make the set, if anyone is interested! When the time
comes to get a much larger list of images, I'll look for one, and if I
can't find it, will do a more robust scraping of internet places to find
them :)

https://github.com/vsoch/singularity-tools/blob/master/docker/makeBases.py

On Fri, Jul 15, 2016 at 2:22 PM, vanessa s <vso...@gmail.com> wrote:

> Hi everyone,
>
> I finished up the command line util to (more easily) convert
> docker2singularity - as you can see below it's pulling images that I don't
> have locally. I'm currently making a bunch of docker images (the core in
> their "library" repo) en masse:
>
> [image: Inline image 1]
>
> and I thought now might be a good time to open up quick discussion about
> where we might want to start sharing these images? Github large file
> storage isn't going to cut it - space runs out almost immediately.
> Singularity Hub (eventually) would be a proper home, but it isn't ready
> now. Currently, my function doesn't do anything to set the running command
> for the container (I was getting the error):
>
> ERROR  : Exec of /bin/sh failed: Exec format error
>
> but when this is worked out, it might be nice to have a (temporary) place
> to put images, even to just inspire thinking about usage. I'm definitely
> happy keeping these on my local machine for now - the reason I'm producing
> them en-masse is so I can package to produce the file/folders lists, and
> start to mess around with how to capture what software is installed /
> different across the different os. I don't think anyone is doing a good job
> of that yet, and it seems important.... who knows what Pokemon are hiding
> inside!
>
> Best,
